style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">赞查（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赞查（藏）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">达日（藏）都是四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县人，藏族牧民，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，二人皆因“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿案”而被阿坝县警方拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名分别重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">臧中美：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年生。吉林省白城法轮功学员。臧中美原是吉林省梨树农场一名小学女教师，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年末因去北京上访被劳教一年半，释放回家后，丈夫和幼小的孩子因经受不住长期的警察上门骚扰被迫离婚。因她不放弃信仰，也被学校开除，流离失所到白城市打工。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，臧中美骑电瓶车宣讲法轮功被白城市洮北区国保大队抓捕，并在其住处抄走大法书籍、电脑、真相资料、现金等物品。后被批捕。曾正在看守所绝食反迫害。臧中美<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月份被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现关押在长春女子监狱十三大队。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">泽让旦真（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生年月不详，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州人，又叫“洛桑丹增”，阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县格尔登寺僧人，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，曾因帮助同寺僧人彭措（又叫平措，已于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日自焚死亡，时年<span lang="EN-US">20</span>岁）以自焚方式（指一种藏人抗议暴政、伸张正义的方式，即藏人自焚者把自己整个奉献出来，以清晰的理智、自愿的心态和惨烈的方式向暴政表达最强烈抗议的无奈选择，以期使公众舆论对极权和高压统治者予以最强烈的谴责或改变对手的情感），纪念中共当局镇压拉萨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>•<span lang="EN-US">14</span>事件三周年，并在阿坝县城洽唐中街实施自焚行动；由于当地僧人和藏人为此举行了大规模情愿示威活动，随与中共军警发生冲突；其随后即被拉萨市警方抓捕、刑拘，并被阿坝藏族羌族自治州马尔康县警方以涉嫌“购买汽油策划，鼓动、帮助自焚罪”执行逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其案在四川省马尔康县法院开庭受审，最终被该法院更换罪名，以“故意杀人罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曾春智：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">45</span>岁。湖北省应城市维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，湖北省应城市维权人士曾春智女士因抗议封城期间物业给居民生活物资配送价格过高而组织居民维权，后遭当局报复，当地警方于<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日竟然对曾春智女士行政拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日当地警方将其刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被应城市检察院批准逮捕。暂无案件进展消息。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曾浩：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东技术师范学院教师、法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年上大学时开始修炼法轮功。曾浩大学毕业后在广州供销学校任教。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共迫害法轮功以来，被开除公职，并两次被非法拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年被迫流离失所近两年。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年仅因为在<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>空间说说中上传和转载了几个与法轮功内容相关的图片，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日在自家楼下买早餐时被广州市海珠区国保大队、江南中街派出所、青葵居委会强行带走并抄家，被非法关押到广州市海珠区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，广州市海珠区法院非法对曾浩进行开庭，律师指出：本案没有受害人，所有指控的证据都是非法的，曾浩无罪。曾浩现任广东技术师范学院天河学院教师，学校盼他早日回校上课。曾浩是家中独子，父母<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁高龄，幼子才<span lang="EN-US">4</span>岁，都需要他照顾。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日曾浩因为在<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>空间转载了几个与神韵、三退相关的图片，被海珠区法院非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曾又梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省聊城市东昌府区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被抓捕抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月庭审。曾又梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曾志远：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南省邵东市（原邵东县）水东江镇牛山村法轮功学员。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，曾志远多次被中共抓捕，三次被劳教，两次被判刑，在看守所、劳教所、监狱共被关押迫害十多年。曾志远<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被邵东市国保大队警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被邵东市法院判刑五年，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬被关押到娄底监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">扎西达杰（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1984</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，四川省甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县人，炉霍寺僧人，中国在押良心犯。因中共当局在西藏及其周边各省涉藏地区强硬推行“爱国和法制宣传教育”活动，引发多地藏民强烈不满，四川省甘孜州炉霍县藏民随于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日（即当年中国农历新年初一）举行大规模和平示威活动；该活动随即遭到中共警方严厉的武力镇压和任意抓捕，致使多人被打死打伤及上百人被抓；至<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，已有<span lang="EN-US">36</span>人被中共当局判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月直至无期徒刑不等的刑期，另有数人被捕后完全失踪；扎西达杰亦因积极参与和平示威游行，于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被警方以“参与和带头示威活动”为由从当地炉霍寺抓走刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县法院以“炉火示威活动的主要带头人”判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。此前被羁押于四川省甘孜藏族自治州康定县监狱；目前在何监狱服刑，情况不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">扎西顿珠（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州若尔盖县唐克镇人。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因独自在四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州若尔盖县城，身披佛教旗帜、手举大幅达赖喇嘛画像，以小跑方式在主要大道上开展抗议中共暴政的示威活动，随被当地警方在极短时间内控制、拘捕；据悉，此前其所在村镇藏民多年来一直因土地遭政府强占、暴力逼迁且得不到任何安置，而多次展开过和平请愿活动（含派代表进省城上访、集体静坐、呈交联署信、集会讨公道等），要求政府当局核实土地征用过程是否非法，并予以公正处理，但却无果而终；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，其被阿坝藏族羌族自治州地方当局正式逮捕，并被判处有期徒刑，罪名、刑期不详，服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">扎西杰（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州若尔盖县人。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，曾因拍录阿坝藏族羌族自治州藏人扎西顿珠身披佛教旗帜、手举大幅达赖喇嘛画像，在若尔盖县城大街上进行抗议中共暴政的抗议过程，并传于网上，随被当地警方于<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日左右抓捕、刑拘，具体罪由不详；据悉，此前其所在乡镇藏民长期因土地问题而被政府强占、暴力逼迁，得不到安置等所困扰，村民多次展开和平请愿活动而无果；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，其与扎西顿珠一起被阿坝藏族羌族自治州地方当局正式逮捕，并被判处有期徒刑，罪名、刑期不详，服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">扎西曲英（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，四川省甘孜州道孚县葛卡乡约呷村人，道孚县尼措寺（全名“尼措图桑达杰林寺”，汉文称“灵雀寺”）僧人，印度西藏甘丹寺强孜经学院最高等级“格西拉然巴”经学博士班一年级学生，藏族政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年前往印度，同年进入印度南部西藏甘丹寺强孜经学院学习。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月下旬持中国驻新德里大使馆发放的旅行证返家探亲过程中，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日突然被中共当局毫无理由地强行拘捕，至此失联。后获悉其被当局指控，因在印度期间曾将道孚县境内发生自焚事件的消息披露给媒体，随被视为泄密。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底，经一位藏族政治犯从监狱获释后向其家人传信，家人方才获知，他和扎西曲英在同一个监狱服刑，扎西曲英被监禁在甘孜州首府康定县新都桥镇的四川省甘孜监狱。后经证实，他于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被四川省甘孜州法院以不知名罪名（疑似“泄露国家机密罪等”）重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">扎西文色（也译：扎西旺楚）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年出生，青海省玉树藏族自治州玉树市人，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Tashi Wangchuk</span>，藏族企业家，藏语言教育倡导者、维权者。十多年来，扎西文色曾先后有两次被当局拘留经历；早年间，曾因“非法前往印度”而被拘捕；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，又因在网上发表抗议政府非法占地的言论而遭拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，因青海、甘肃等省的藏区公立中学已停止使用藏语授课，仅将其作为一门母语课程，甚至有些学校完全不授藏语课，引起藏人不满，与此同时，其所在青海省玉树市结古街道办事处亦开始明令禁止当地寺院及私立学校向僧侣以外的民众传授藏语，于是其便在微博上公开发表了对藏语教育逐步被丧失的担忧，此举很快引起当局不满与警觉。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，为敦促各级政府自觉兑现、维护藏语言合法使用及地位的承诺，其开始上访北京，向中央递交检举信函，揭露藏区地方政府并未支持藏人语言教育的事实，并接受纽约时报记者采访，制作了一个为时<span lang="EN-US">9</span>分钟的视频短片，此举进一步遭致地方政府仇视与嫉恨。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，因其在微博群里再次呼吁，建议青海省人大会议应该敦促地方政府提升双语教育，并雇用更多的会说双语的地方官员，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日即被玉树市警方以涉嫌“危害国家安全”刑拘，后被玉树市检察院以“煽动分裂国家罪”正式批捕，并被移交到地方法院。一直被羁押于青海省玉树州看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，扎西文色涉嫌煽动分裂国家案宣判，青海玉树州中级法院判处扎西文色<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">翟国兴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">天津法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日早晨在天津河东区万新村菜市场讲法轮功，被警察抓捕到东新派出所。当天中午抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月翟国兴被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月关押到天津女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">翟亚男：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，合肥庐阳区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，<a name="_Hlk52326366">翟亚男</a>发放真相资料，被蜀山区井岗派出所警察抓捕，后被关押于合肥女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，翟亚男被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并勒索处罚金三千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">辽宁省绥中县人，法轮功学员。因信仰、宣传法轮功遭多次打压逼迫。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被辽宁省绥中县警方以涉邪教罪刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被转正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日其案在辽宁省绥中县法院开庭受审，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”一审判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。其不服，已上诉到葫芦岛市中级法院，律师递交了开庭申请，即将面临二审。目前被羁押于绥中县看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">詹传云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安徽省长丰县女访民。其家房屋被拆迁、土地被征收，因未获合理补偿而上访。詹传云女士是于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被警方从家中抓捕后刑拘羁押于合肥女子看守所的，被羁押<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天才开庭审理。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，詹传云被敲诈勒索（政府）罪案件在长丰县人民法院第二法庭开庭审理，詹传云女士的律师作了无罪辩护，合肥市<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多位访民到庭旁听案件审理。据悉，案件审理时，公诉人提出的证据被律师驳回，女访民岂能敲诈政府？尤其是敲诈国家暴力机器公安部门，案件审理将结束时，迫于证据难以支持敲诈勒索罪的法官问被告人詹传云，撤掉敲诈勒索罪变更为寻衅滋事罪行不行？被告人詹传云女士非常坚定的回答，她没有罪。最后陈述时，詹传云女士称自己为自己家房屋被拆迁和土地征收上访维权，她没有罪。最终，法院仍判处詹传云<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk52187221"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日与好友周玉香和周君一起到平度仁兆赶集，被仁兆派出所警察抓捕。后，<a name="_Hlk52323834">展中香</a>和周玉香分别被判<span class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">战玉彩：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New lang="EN-US">30</span>周年临近，中共当局的维稳镇压措施愈来愈严厉，北京民主维权人士张宝成也被抓捕、抄家。据张宝成妻子刘珏帆介绍：“北京时间<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>：<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分张宝成“寻衅滋事、宣扬恐怖主义、极端主义”案在北京市第二中级法院<span lang="EN-US">A</span>座第<span lang="EN-US">12</span>法庭开庭 。未当庭宣判。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张朝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张成武：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东潍坊市昌乐县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日下午，昌乐县马宋镇张家庄村张成武在家中被警察绑架。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被山东青州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张春蕾：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西忻州法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，张春蕾因要求各级政府公开关于迫害法轮功的政策而被非法抓捕。后被批捕，起诉。罪名是利用邪教破坏法律实施罪。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午忻州市忻府区法院开庭审理张春蕾利用邪教破坏法律实施案，文东海律师作为辩护律师参与开庭审理，该案检察院不让辩护律师阅卷，不接收辩护律师手续，不听取辩护律师意见。到了法院仍然不允许阅卷，不公开审理，没有庭审录音录像，在庭上只有法官检察官可以看卷，辩护律师和被告人均不让看卷，辩护律师拒绝就检察官口头念的证据目录发表质证意见，申请回避驳回，要求复议法官认为没有复议权利。后遭判刑，刑期不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张迪</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵文静、黄金桔、吕月霞、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日该教会一座兴建中的教堂，遭到数百名政府人员强拆，双方发生争执，教会物品被毁坏，信徒被打伤，数十人包括该<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名负责人被公安带走，后这<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连得。目前，所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，该教会成立<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张冬宁：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1997</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，安徽省淮南市人，漫画师，曾赴日本创作，“猪头人身”系列漫画作品创作者，中国在押政治犯。近年来，因以中国大陆发生的诸多热点新闻事件为背景，创作出<span lang="EN-US">300</span>余幅“猪头人身”系列漫画作品，随引起社会广泛热议，但却触怒了中共当局脆弱的政治敏感神经，招致当权者极度忌恨与恶意打击；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，在其从日本持旅游签证回国之后，很快就被安徽省淮南市田家庵区警方莫名抓捕、刑拘，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被地方检察院以其漫画作品涉及“辱华”为罪由正式批捕，并指控其创作“猪头人身”系列漫画行为是刻意歪曲中国历史，曲解社会热点新闻事件，违反了中国相关法律；据悉，已被当局列为“精日”分子（“精日”系一种网络流行语，即精神日本人的简称，又称为精日分子，在中国大陆政治和社会议题中属于负面指涉用语，专指极端崇拜日本军国主义仇恨自身民族、在精神上将自己视同军国主义日本人的非日籍人群），其案被当局视为境内外“精日”分子合作利用互联网实施“辱华”违法犯罪活动之案件；截至目前，尚无更多具体信息。目前被羁押于淮南市看守所（安徽省淮南市田家庵区安成镇黑泥洼村石家店，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">232038</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张桂芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">哈尔滨市通河县法轮功学员，哈尔滨医科大学本科毕业，本是通河县妇幼保健院主治医师，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年，开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日早，公安局一张桂芝和另一位法轮功学员被绑架。后张桂芝被判刑五年，在黑龙江省女子监狱遭受迫害，曾经被关小号，戴脚镣。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，张桂芝在通河县邮政局邮寄劝善信，邮局工作人员拒邮后，说要请示一下领导。接着“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”国保大队五人，抓捕了张桂芝。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，哈尔滨市依兰县第三法院对张桂芝庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月获知，张桂芝被哈尔滨市依兰县第三法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张国兵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东河源维权人士。张国兵有两个孩子的，曾于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日以学生家长身份依法申请公布学校食品安全监督信息。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">8</span>时被东源县公安带走，约三小时后被广东河源市公安局人员抄家。搜走手机、身份证、护照、银行卡等物（张没有电脑）。家属两次都问公安人员，是什么事抓人？均回答，不知道，查清楚再说。后获悉<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪名被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日广东省河源县法院以寻衅滋事罪判处张国兵有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，没收作案工具苹果手机<span lang="EN-US">1</span>部，<span lang="EN-US">NOKIA</span>牌手机<span lang="EN-US">1</span>部。 判决依据的所谓犯罪事实是，张国兵多次翻墙使用推待和注册使用微信发表和转发一些涉嫌不实和诋毁国家党政领导人、抨击国家制度的负面言论信息，造成严重的不良社会影响。张国兵刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张海涛</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年出生，河南省南阳市镇平县籍人，原<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代国企下岗工人，新疆区域电信产品销售者、自由职业者，民主人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被新疆维吾尔族自治区乌鲁木齐市中亚南路派出所警方以涉嫌“煽动民族仇恨、民族歧视罪”抄家、刑事拘留、逮捕；之后被以“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕，羁押于新疆乌鲁木齐市看守所。据悉，其家中银行卡全部被警方冻结，妻子即将生育，生活面临极大困境。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日再次被变更罪名以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”继续超期关押，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被乌鲁木齐中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家罪”、“为境外刺探、非法提供情报罪”重判徒刑<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，剥权<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处没收个人财产人民币<span lang="EN-US">12</span>万；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日经新疆乌鲁木齐高级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判。目前在新疆维吾尔族自治区沙雅监狱九监区服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张华<span lang="EN-US">: </span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东威海荣成市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年六十岁。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日清晨，张华在她母亲家中被警察团团围住，被抓走。后张华被非法关押在文登看守所。在看守所被非法关押里，张华被迫害的大脑混沌不清，什么也想不起来。而张华的父母均有残疾，她父亲曾经干过生产队长、村会计、大队书记，临老因劳致残，伤了腰和腿，不能行走，却连个残疾证都没办上；她母亲九十度弯腰，也不能直立行走。俩位八十多岁的老人最敢怒不敢言，只能默默承受。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被关押到济南女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张贾龙</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：<span lang="EN-US">1988</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日出生，贵州省贵阳市人，前腾讯财经频道编辑，网络活跃推手和博客作者，民主异见公民，中国在押政治犯。曾因报导过艾未未工作室被强拆新闻，关注及报导过“结石宝宝之父”赵连海等维权信息而广为社会热议；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，曾因在推特上发“今天在出租车上听司机说五一期间<span lang="EN-US">2/3</span>的北京出租车司机将举行罢工”推文，被北京警方传唤<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时并抄家；后又因“在境外推特网站发布虚假信息并被转发<span lang="EN-US">37</span>次，扰乱社会秩序”，被北京警方视为“重、特大敏感性案件”，是“在互联网上鼓吹罢工”、“企图制造事端，妨害首都公交治安秩序的危险分子”，随被处以<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日行政拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，曾因就互联网自由问题而在北京会见时任美国国务卿约翰·克里，会谈中因直言希望美国政府能帮助中国人拆除防火长城，谴责美国公司帮助中国当局限制互联网自由，担忧刘晓波、许志永等良心犯、人权活动人士的狱中生存境况，随后又在《外交政策》上发文称“我想告诉克里的所有事”，呼吁美国拒绝发给中国负责防火长城的相关人员签证（含北京邮电大学校长兼防火长城创建人之一方滨兴），随引起当局极度不快和警觉；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其被腾讯公司以“泄露商业秘密等敏感信息行为”为由解聘，真实理由皆因与克里会见提及刘晓波等，及经常在网上公布中共中央宣传部指令；后其为求谋生返回家乡贵阳市低调生活，近期新婚不久刚产下幼女；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日突然被辖区警方及维稳办人员从家中带走，并被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；据悉，其已有较长时间未发表令人关注的公众言论，其微信圈发声亦不频繁，对当前许多热点问题无特别重要评论，维权网友疑指仍与之前会见克里之事有关，或与一个多月前他与友人饭聚、及近期关于香港抗议的媒体言论有关，当局欲拿他几年前的推特言论相威胁；因其莫名被抓，其妻及幼女生活顿陷困境，需要更多人关注。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，张贾龙涉嫌寻衅滋事案今在贵阳开庭，张贾龙坚称无罪，而律师也均做无罪辩护，当庭未宣判。目前被羁押于贵阳市南明区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张荆州：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生，原湖北省荆州市金隆集团公司员工，法轮功学员。因修炼法轮功，张荆州已被处罚<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次：<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚上，荆州市公安局指挥，沙市开发区公安局和燎原派出所十几个警察在出租屋，抓捕了张荆州与邵廉，并抄家，抢走打印纸<span lang="EN-US">2</span>十多箱，打印机约<span lang="EN-US">4</span>、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>台，电脑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>台，还有裁纸刀等物品。张荆州、邵廉被关押在荆州西门看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，张荆州被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，并勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；邵廉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张君</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：四川省人，在重庆市巴南区工作，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年左右开始信仰、修炼法轮功，但之后很快即遭到当局的严酷打压。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，当他在重庆市巴南区跳石镇给村民讲述法轮功被无辜迫害的真相时，很快就遭到跳石镇派出所警方的抓捕、刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其案在重庆市巴南区法院第一次开庭审理。但由于原告公诉人无法出示有效证据，律师提出不合法律程序，法院庭审被迫中止。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，其案被第二次开庭受审，尽管律师为其作了有力的无罪辩护，面对律师的质询和辩护，公诉人承认其实他们没有任何证据可以证明法轮功是“邪教”，也找不到任何法律法规说法轮功是“邪教”，但是在法庭无任何有效证据的情况下，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日其依然已被重庆市巴南区法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”非法秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。其不服提已起上诉，目前被羁押在重庆市巴南区看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张君琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年生，宁夏固原市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共恶党开始疯狂迫害法轮功，张君琴因坚持修炼，遭受中共邪党抓捕、关押、劳教，而后被迫流离失所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，流离失所<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年多，回家不久的张君琴女士，被固原市原州区国保大队警察抓捕，被关押迫害<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月获悉，张君琴被固原市原州区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张亢<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">云南玉溪市法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">.</span>毕业于西南师范大学，二零一五年八月份，参加玉溪华宁教育系统考试合格，考取华宁县的教师岗位，二零一五年九月，到华宁县偏远山区彝族苗族自治县通红甸乡华宁第九中学担任中学语文教师。张亢因为坚持信仰法轮功，不写所谓的“三书”，华宁县第九中学校领导，在华宁县教育局不法人员的授意下，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，以一年满为借口，解聘张亢老师。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日其母亲任惠萍发法轮功真相资料，被绑架到红塔分局。当天深夜十一点多，玉溪市红塔分局国保大队到任会萍家，抄家，警察以打印机是张亢的为借口，在凌晨一点多，抓捕了张亢及抢走家里的私人物品。任惠萍、张亢母女俩被非法关押在红塔区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被玉溪市江川县法院视频开庭，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日任惠萍、张亢均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张莉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西南昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份，南昌市西湖区公安分局与东湖区公安分局联合，成立了迫害法轮功学员的专案组。他们通过摄像头查找后进行抓捕、抄家，分别于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日逐一抓捕了张莉、江兰英、张文涛、胡水英、陈宝芝。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，江西省南昌市西湖区法院判法轮功学员张莉有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张立娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林伊通县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，吉林省伊通县法轮功学员张立娟和她儿子曹博宇分别在自家附近和家中被吉林省辽源市国保警察马队长等人秘密抓捕，关押在辽源市看守所。警察又抄家，劫走法轮功书籍、法相、资料、电脑、打印机、订书器等大量私人物品。曹博宇被关押近<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月左右被放回。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，辽源市西安区法院视频开庭，张立娟被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">黑龙江省双鸭山法轮功学员、双鸭山市石油公司职工、法轮功学员张立君女，<span lang="EN-US">51</span>岁，据因给公检法警察邮寄法轮功宣传信，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被双鸭山市公安局、尖山分局等单位抓捕，羁押在双鸭山市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日遭双鸭山尖山检察院批捕。卷宗目前打回尖山分局补充侦查。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张莉敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省本溪市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，胡林被转往沈阳法库县看守所关押。胡林最终被判刑两年。从被抓捕开始，胡林一直在绝食抵制迫害，在被迫害的生命垂危的情况下，被法库县看守所走后门强行送往沈阳康家山监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被沈阳康家山监狱迫害致死。本案<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日宣判：邓玉林和杨丽威<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，各罚金二万元，张莉敏<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万五千元，张鹏柱<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，勒索罚金一万元。张莉敏刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张乃君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New lang="EN-US">17</span>日，当其在鞍山市铁西区兴盛街道附近粘贴法轮功资料时，遭到铁西区兴盛街道办事处工作人员白英涛的恶意举报，遂被鞍山市铁西区兴盛派出所警方很快以涉嫌宣传邪教罪抓捕，次日被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日已被鞍山市铁西区检察院以同罪名正式批捕。被羁押于鞍山市第一看守所。后取保获释。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日又遭抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被庭审。刑期未知。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; lang="EN-US">25</span>日，胡林被转往沈阳法库县看守所关押。胡林最终被判刑两年。从被抓捕开始，胡林一直在绝食抵制迫害，在被迫害的生命垂危的情况下，被法库县看守所走后门强行送往沈阳康家山监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被沈阳康家山监狱迫害致死。本案<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日宣判：邓玉林和杨丽威<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，各罚金二万元，张莉敏<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张勤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">上海法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，家住上海市徐汇区，原是上海市胜德塑料有限公司的技术骨干，曾任总工程师、质监科科长等职务。一九九四年九月开始修炼法轮。张勤因为坚持信仰曾经两次被判刑，刑期分别为<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，还被劳教迫害<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，张勤又遭逮捕抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日下午，张勤被上海奉贤区法院庭审、判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，借口是“累犯重判”。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张勤：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1942</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，河北遵化市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，遵化多个村镇的数十名法轮功学员几乎同时在凌晨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点多遭到警察的入室抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日张勤被遵化市法院宣判<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">,</span></b>被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张清香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西太原市老年法轮功学员。太原市公安局迎泽分局警察<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日非法闯民宅，抄家抓捕法轮功学员孙志芬（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、王素平（<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁）、罗保军（<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁）、张清香（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）、张润英（<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁）、郭润鲜（<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁）、田玉琴（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、胡兰英（<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁），其中多数是老太太。山西省太原市这八位老年法轮功学员被非法关押近一年后得知被迎泽区法院非法判刑、勒索罚款，并被劫持到监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张仁光<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男 ，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">64</span>岁，辽宁省大连市沙河口区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日晚九点左右，张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波四人因发真相资料，分别被国保和民权派出所绑架。在张仁光家抄走大量耗材。后全送姚家看守所。大连市沙河口区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日庭审法轮功学员张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波，并判张仁光<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、勒索罚款两万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张三曼：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市金州区石河镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚，谷秀华（女）、刘希永（男）、周兴（男）、李天学（男）、王丽志（女）、张三曼（女）、谭春荣（女）、孙宝英（女）、刘井龙（男），去大连市金普新区炮台镇袁屯村发放新书《共产主义的终极目的》，被炮台镇派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午二在大连市金州法院庭审。后谷秀华、周兴、王丽志，被大连市金州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；张三曼、谭春荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，李天学被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刘希永、孙宝英、刘井龙的情况还不清楚。张三曼刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张少杰：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1965</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，河南省南乐县人，前河南省南乐县基督教三自爱国运动委员会主席、基督教协会会长，第九届南乐县政协委员，南乐县基督教会牧师，中国在押良心犯。长期以来，因其身为牧师，经常帮助弱势群体维权解难，尤其是当信徒的合法权益受到侵害时，均想法给予及时的帮助与维权，随在当地备受信徒的喜爱，但这种行为却与政府某些人的利益发生冲突，随遭到当局的强烈不满和忌恨；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被南乐县警方在无任何法律手续的前提下强行从教会带走，其两个胞妹在众人的陪同下前去公安局要人，也被警察强行带走，其余人等亦遭警方堵截和殴打，之后才得知张少杰已被当地警方以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，又被追加涉嫌“妨害公务罪”予以批捕，但在起诉书中又显示将“妨害公务罪”变更为“诈骗罪”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，终被河南省南乐县法院以“诈骗罪”和“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。此前曾先后被羁押在河南省南乐县看守所和濮阳市看守所；目前在河南省新乡市河南第二监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张淑琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江伊春市法轮功学员，女，</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1951</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">，家住伊春市伊春区，在伊春经营一家旅店。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日当地警方对张淑琴经营的旅店进行搜查，并以「利用×教组织破坏法律实施罪」将张淑琴刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，将张淑琴批准逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日伊美区法院对张淑琴开庭审理。张淑琴本人没有到法庭现场，是在看守所以视频方式出庭。律师为张淑琴做了无罪辩护。张淑琴女儿刘春莉也为母亲做了无罪辩护。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张水兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日生，云岭通信器材公司退休职工。张水兰<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年曾经遭受<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年冤狱迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日散发法轮功真相资料遭恶人诬告，被昆明市盘龙区东华派出所警察抓捕、非法抄家，抢走平板计算机一台，及大法书籍、数据等私人物品。后张水兰被昆明市西山区检察院起诉，云南省昆明市西山区法院<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日对昆明市法轮功学员张水兰判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10000</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张素华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">吉林省通化市东昌区法轮功学员，女性，<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁。张素华是<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被通化市警察绑架的，在被非法关押一年半后，于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，在未通知本人律师的情况下被非法开庭的。家属从接到通知到开庭也才不足三小时。当天下午一点半，对张素华非法庭审，整个过程仅用了十分钟，草草收场。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，吉林省通化市东昌区法院对张素华非法判刑七年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张树德：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">28</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">岁，哈尔滨市双城区新兴乡人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。自幼练习和笃信法轮功。哈尔滨工业大学毕业后，曾应聘于大连理工设计院，后外派到盘锦市高新技术产业开发区工作，是个诚实、可信、敬业的好青年。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，因居住证到期，张树德到所在地的兴隆台区兴盛派出所办理顺延手续时，当身份证录入相关信息时，警察问他有什么信仰，他称其信仰法轮功，随被拒绝办理居住证，并被威胁要对他调查。三天后，其居室遭搜查，本人被传唤做笔录。<span lang="EN-US"> 6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被双手戴着手铐非法送到盘锦市中心医院检查身体，然后就被强行刑拘于盘锦看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，他被盘锦市公安局兴隆台区分局正式逮捕，并将其案移交到兴隆台区检察院。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，检察院案将其案卷移交到兴隆台区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其案被盘锦市兴隆台区法院开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，张树德被该法院一审枉法重判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。其不服上诉。其所在家乡的亲友得知其被冤判后，立刻决定伸出援手征签营救，同乡的父老乡亲们在极短的时间里，亲自填写上自己的名字或按下红手印，呼吁无罪释放张树德回家，目前已有<span lang="EN-US">1744</span>人签名声援。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张顺新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">新疆喀什地区泽普县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">53</span>岁，在中共对法轮功持续至今近二十年的迫害中，他因修炼法轮功在<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，但他挺过来了。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出狱回家。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日晚十点左右，张顺新被塔西南石油基地公安局（隶属于泽普县公安局）警察冯海洋骗到派出所后，再次被绑架关押抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，新疆喀什地区公安局警察到法轮功学员张顺新家通知亲属，张顺新现被关在农三师图木舒克市盖米里克监狱。亲属这才知道张顺新于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，并在亲属、律师不在场的情况下秘密宣判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张涛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">澳门居民。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，珠海王家婚礼教会牧师魏小妹及丈夫李炳新、同工张涛（澳门居民）被捕。数个月后，珠海市香洲区检察院以“诈骗罪”起诉。控方指魏小妹、李炳新及张涛涉嫌诈骗信徒奉献款，购买房产，构成诈骗罪。据知情人士披露，当局的指控缺乏有力证据，难以成立。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，香洲区民族宗教事务局取缔该教会，并扣留该教会近五十台电脑<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b><span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，当局出动数十名公安，拘捕该教会十多名信徒，经过连续审讯及威胁，信徒被迫写下不利于教会领袖的证词。警方最终以诈骗罪刑事拘留该教会牧师魏小妹及丈夫李炳新、同工张涛。据知情人士披露，该案由珠海市政法委督办。当局先以“邪教罪”调查此案，但因查无实据，又改为“诈骗罪”问罪，这明显是一起宗教案件。目前，广东珠海王家婚礼教会牧师魏小妹及丈夫李炳新、同工张涛（澳门居民）三人，被珠海市香洲区检察院以“诈骗罪”起诉至法院，指当事人诈骗奉献款，上述三人面临判刑。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张廷福：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，<span lang="EN-US">70</span>多岁老人张廷福在达州下火车，被达州车站派出所拦截扣押后刑事拘留，问其原因，是重庆上清寺派出所将张廷福上传为网上追逃人员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日重庆维权人士张廷福，被重庆市公安局渝中区分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑拘，现羁押在渝中区看守所。家属经多方投诉后，才于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日拿到刑事拘留通知书，张廷福也从达州转至重庆渝中区看守所，得知成为逃犯的原因，是派出所以其涉嫌寻衅滋事罪，上传为网上追逃。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张文斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">原籍山东、原定今年大学毕业。因<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日在微信实名公开发布“习近平下课”、“共产党下课”视频后，其微信被封杀，后又遭强迫失踪，目前处于失联状态。此前他曾因言获罪被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天。张文斌说，自己挺身而出，武汉肺炎疫情是导火索。而这段矛头指向习近平的视频使他又遭遇了强迫失踪。目前没有进一步的信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张文涛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西南昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份，南昌市西湖区公安分局与东湖区公安分局联合，成立了迫害法轮功学员的专案组。他们通过摄像头查找后进行抓捕、抄家，分别于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日逐一抓捕了张莉、江兰英、张文涛、胡水英、陈宝芝。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，江西省南昌市西湖区法院判法轮功学员张文涛<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US"> 2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张五洲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">人权捍卫者、湖北籍、家住广东清远市。张五洲是被关进广州白云区看守所死亡的张六毛的姐姐。张五洲为了给弟弟的不明死亡讨回公道受到打压，开始关注公益和参与一些民主、人权活动。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，广州女律师孙世华在广州荔湾区华林派出所办案时，受到该所民警殴打并遭脱衣检查侮辱。随行的张五洲和梁颂基作为目击者，在网上公开为孙世华作证。广州警方为此报复，以“寻衅滋事罪”抓捕了张五洲和梁颂基。后梁颂基被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半和张五洲<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。张五洲女士于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日当天，前往广州著名风景区白云山，在山上栏杆上打出横幅，上书“勿忘六世，撤回恶法”、“女律师被殴目击证人”等字样，以此纪念<span lang="EN-US">31</span>年前的六四事件，以及反对中共两会刚刚通过的香港国安法的实施。张五洲把该活动拍照及视频发微信朋友圈和其它平台发布后，翌日（<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日）下午<span lang="EN-US">14</span>时<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分，广东清远市公安局清城区分局石角派出所以张五洲“涉嫌扰乱公共秩序”为由将其清远市家中传唤带走，随后被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日来警方又来抄家。后狱中遭受极其残暴的酷刑虐待。张五洲案于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日在清远市清城区法院开庭，未当庭宣判。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张希明：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市东丽区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日上午九点三十分，天津市东丽区分局警察、国保大队便衣、军粮城派出所警察共十几个人，闯入张希明家中，强行非法抄家，并抓捕了<a name="_Hlk52324773">张希明</a>与他母亲刘玉红。当天下午五点，警察把刘玉红放回家，当晚把张希明关押到东丽区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，军粮城派出所两个警察给刘玉红送来张希明被刑事拘留的通知书。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月底被开庭，后获悉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁左右，大连市中山区人，原中山区青云小学教师，法轮功学员，良心犯。因信仰法轮功并起诉江泽民，曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，被送洗脑班<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日在学校上班时间又被大连市国保与民主广场派出所警方联合绑架抓走，家被查抄，电脑及相关法轮功资料等均被搜走。其丈夫孙俊区派出所问询，已被扣押，后得知夫妇二人均被关押在大连市姚家看守所羁押。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其被大连中山区检察院以涉嫌“邪教罪”正式批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年被大连市中山区法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”秘密判处<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月。其不服提起上诉，大连市中级法院未经二审即对她维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底，张霞被送往辽宁省女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张小麦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">原名陈煜，浙江临海市基督徒。张小麦</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">(</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈煜）因在开设网上书店“小麦书房”销售基督教书籍</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">,</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月被捕</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">,</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">在张小麦于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月被中共当局以「网上销售非法境外宗教出版物」被捕后，公安部曾通报全国，要求各地国保根据从「小麦书房」搜到的发货订单接触收货人，就其购买书籍的取向和「当地非法宗教活动的情况」进行取证，有上万人被问询。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">27</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日一审判决，以非法经营罪判</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">7</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年有期徒刑。并处以罚金</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万，所扣押</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12864</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本书予以销毁。判决书同时裁定，被告除了被罚</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万元外，还须追缴售书违法所得的</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万元上缴国库，无法追缴的，由被告退赔，并须予判决生效后十天内缴纳。这是对传播基督教的基督徒的赤裸裸的镇压。刑期至：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2026</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">9</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张小平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">洛阳维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>号，洛阳政府为了修建西环路，在程序不合法的情况下，对张小平家宅基地上的房屋进行了强拆，张小平也因此被逼自学法律，走上了依法维权抗争之路。张小平通过信息公开、行政诉讼等法律途径获取了一些关于修建道路的政府信息，通过对这些信息的分析，发现了前洛阳市市长郭洪昌、李柳身违法修建西环路造成至少<span lang="EN-US">1</span>亿元国有资产流失的事实。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，张小平就这一事实，实名向驻河南中央第一巡视组<span lang="EN-US">65</span>号邮寄了一封《举报信》，此信查询单显示<span lang="EN-US">3.28</span>日已经妥投。巡视组不但没有保护张小平举报人的身份，此举更是将张小平暴露在被举报人的眼皮之下，被打击报复也是迟早之事； 因为举报的事情，张小平接到过威胁电话。关于泄漏举报人信息的问题，张小平通过新浪微博发声质疑，并要求相关部门查处。其最后一个博文发于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，结果，违法人员没得到查处，举报人却被抓了进去。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，洛阳公民张小平疑因举报厅级干部被刑事拘留，其丈夫张智斌行政拘留。原因疑是他们向中央巡视组举报原洛阳市市长郭洪昌、李柳身（正厅级干部）。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，张小平被洛阳公安局南昌路分局（电话<span lang="EN-US">0379-64316110</span>）抓捕；涉嫌罪名是“寻衅滋事”，<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日早被刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被批捕。羁押在洛阳看守所。后无进一步信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张绪民：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">男，山东泰安肥城市法轮功学员、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十四岁，原肥城市国土资源局副局长。因坚持修炼法轮功被非法劳教两年、冤判四年六个月。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被肥城市公安局拘留，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被批捕。张绪民被关押在肥城市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，山东泰安肥城市法院判张绪民被<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款三万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张雪春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">微信名海燕，维权人士。于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被沈阳市和平分局以（聚众犹乱社会秩序）罪刑拘，目前关押在沈阳市第一看守所，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日批捕。张雪春家人委托的代理律师向大家征集在北京最高检察院、最高人民法院的目击证人，证明张雪春在按照我国相关法律法规，依法有序向最高人民检察院，最高人民法院，提出司法改革建议过程中，没有任何违法行为，更没有任何犯罪行为以事实，然后走正常法律程序，还当事人以清白，请大家自愿报名，为张雪春出庭作证，证明其当事人无罪。已有上百人目击者报名上庭作证。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张艳华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省长春市法轮功学员。张艳华<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月遭长春净月开发区派出所警察绑架，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份遭净月开发区法院非法庭审，被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并遭非法罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<a name="_Hlk52056887"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></a></span></p> <span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52056887;"></span> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">张永宝</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：辽宁省鞍山市人，法轮功信仰者。因信仰、宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日晚在高俊的七岭子家中，张永宝、高俊、、二人被辽阳公安局警察跟踪绑架、构陷，后经辽阳县法院三次庭审，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日二人被一审以犯“邪教罪”分别冤判有期徒刑。其中，高俊被重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其不服已提起上诉。张永宝被冤判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">张玉明：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1955</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，河北遵化市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，遵化多个村镇的数十名法轮功学员几乎同时在凌晨<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点多遭到警察的入室抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日张玉明被遵化市法院宣判<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">,</span></b>被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">6000</span>元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张元华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川泸州市纳溪区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年四十八岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日上午，四川泸州市七名法轮功学员高贤英、董国珍、周明英、张元华、刘忠芬、帅先芳、宋平（男）驱车到泸州市合江县五通镇赶场，被派出所警察抓捕，然后带到合江九支镇派出所审问。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月取保候审。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被四川泸州市合江县法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，处罚金六千。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张展</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年代出生，陕西省籍人，上海市浦东新区常驻居民，网络异见人士，公民记者、民主公民。硕士学位，毕业后即在上海谋职工作；因不满中共政府的政治现状，长期在网络平台发布批评“一党专政”、腐败滥权等言论，其做派活跃、内容尖锐而颇具针对性，故而曾多次被上海市警方约谈、传唤及威胁；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年以来，因其在微信等网络平台大量转发香港“反送中”抗议视频及文图资料，尤其是每天自己撰文发声，利用行为艺术等为声援香港举牌，随于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被上海警方传唤，自此失联，后知其被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，其父因受警方威胁，故对外拒透其具体信息；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，终获释放；据悉，羁押期间，其曾被两次做强制性“精神病鉴定”。此前被羁押于上海市浦东新区看守所。张展自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日左右去到武汉报导当地疫情，一直在微信、推特、<span lang="EN-US">YouTube </span>等社交媒体平台上直播武汉的现场情况，并尽其所能地帮助受疫情影响的人维权。张展在武汉实地写了大量关于武汉疫情的真实报道。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在武汉遭“强迫失踪”，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被上海市浦东分局刑事拘留，被控罪名是寻衅滋事，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月遭正式逮捕。被起诉，其在狱中绝食抗议，身体状况极差。现羁押在浦东新区看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，张展女士案一审开庭，并当庭宣判，张展女士因言获罪被上海浦东新区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张正廷：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省丹东市经济合作开发区访民、台属。张正廷于<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年投资于丹东市振兴区浪头镇的顺达微孔过滤器厂，到<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，张正廷投资的厂房恰好在丹东市城区公路扩建规划内而需要搬迁。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，地方政府在无任何手续的情况下，出动公安、城管以及社会人员几百号人，对张正廷的顺达过滤器厂层层包围，将厂房夷为平地。张正廷的妻子宋玉洁还被殴打致伤。正是在地方申诉无望的情况下，张正廷、宋玉洁夫妻才不得已进京告御状。想不到，这一告就是<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个年头，且每年的敏感时期都要被维稳，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年十八大前夕，丹东市政府提出给张正廷、宋玉洁夫妇俩<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元维稳补偿费，张正廷拒绝后被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。如此政府却诬陷其为敲诈勒索。张正廷今年已经<span lang="EN-US">76</span>岁，其在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日凌晨零点<span lang="EN-US">48</span>分，被辽宁省丹东市驻京维稳人员<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余人，闯入其位于北京市大兴区的暂住地，强行截回辽宁丹东。后被丹东市经济合作开发区公安分局刑拘，理由是张正廷涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被正式逮捕。羁押在丹东市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张志江：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赤峰市元宝山区五家镇小石头分金桥村居民，法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日晚在大水清道上被喀喇沁旗楼子店派出所警察绑架。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日上午，赤峰元宝山区五家镇村警李文明领着锦山公安局警察闯到张志江家非法抄家，在家里没人的情况下，搜走了大法书。并将张志江非法关押在喀喇沁旗锦山看守所。之后，喀喇沁旗公安局编造材料，将构陷张志江的案卷上报到喀喇沁旗检察院，检察院以张志江炼法轮功、悬挂真相条幅等理由，非法起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，内蒙古赤峰市喀喇沁旗法院开庭非法庭审法轮功学员张志江。张志江为自己做了无罪辩护。法院随后将张志江非法判刑，具体刑期不详。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵帮海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川成都法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，成都市法轮功学员赵帮海、李常秋夫妇因宣传法轮功而被抓捕。后均遭枉判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑，那年他们的独生女儿十六岁。四年来，失去父母照顾的独生女儿多次要求会见冤狱中的父亲，却遭监狱无情的推诿、拒绝。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵晨宇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">昆明市女教师、法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十五岁，原是昆明市第三十中学一级教师，中文系研究生，是一位学生爱戴的好老师。赵晨宇曾于<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。赵晨宇于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初回西双版纳傣族自治州景洪市探望年迈的母亲，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日刚返回到昆明家中，就被跟踪而来的西双版纳景洪市国保大队警察抓捕、抄家。于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日在西双版纳再次被庭审，判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。被关押在西双版纳傣族自治州景洪市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">赵春侠</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，辽宁省辽阳市人，基督徒，辽阳市朝光村基督教家庭教会会计。因其教会为基督教家庭教会，且不愿到中共当局指定的“三自”教会敬拜、聚会，遂遭致当局的严打惩罚；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其被辽阳市太子河区警方突然抓捕刑拘，并被指控教会内部使用了基督徒信仰灵修崇拜书籍及相关印刷品，并在教会的便利店销往其他省市，属于非法买卖行为；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被辽宁省辽阳市太子河区法院以“非法经营罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。目前被羁押于辽阳市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">赵鄂川：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">贵州省贵阳市法轮功学员。赵鄂川<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被警察绑架。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点至<span lang="EN-US">11</span>点半遭贵阳市南明区法院被庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，南明区法院告知律师，对赵鄂川判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。赵鄂川提出上诉。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，律师已经把赵鄂川的上诉状递交到贵阳市中级法院。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span
