style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">上期名单刑满释放人员共<span lang="EN-US">17</span>人名单及简介<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈永明、高亨柏、韩良、胡光珍、</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">李纪凤、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李先利、李秀芬、连燕、</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">林丽芳、</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘瑞虎、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">裘小平、单丽娜、王好梅</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、吴海波</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、袁琼秀、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">张凤琴</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、钟怡君</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、陈永明</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：新疆轮台县第三中学校长。陈永明于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被抓，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月即以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。中共当局指控陈永明的罪状极尽荒唐，比如说陈“在公共场所（中学教师大会）发表所谓‘普世价值观’、‘民主宪政’等言论，起哄闹事，造成公共秩序严重混乱，“推号<span lang="EN-US">@crude_prude</span>关注反党分子推特帐号<span lang="EN-US">335</span>个”，手机收藏反党照片。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、高亨柏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省青岛市平度市法轮功学员。山东平度市法院于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日将法轮功学员高亨柏判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑。山东省青岛法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月又高亨柏上诉案维持原判。高亨柏住在山东平度市南村镇（原兰底镇）小阵村。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，高亨柏在兰底镇集市上向老百姓免费赠送<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年新年台历，宣传法轮大法，被不明真相的人恶告。随后兰底派出所警察绑架了高亨柏，当天上午，兰底派出所警察到高亨柏家非法抄家。后被关押在平度市门村看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">3</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、韩良：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆公民，韩良系<span lang="EN-US">49</span>年生人，现已年过七旬。他自称是国军军官后代，长期游走街头讲抗战史，讲历史真相，宣传法治人权。因与官方的版本有出入而受到重庆公安打压。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，韩良曾因上街纪念“抗战胜利<span lang="EN-US">68</span>周年”被公安打伤。去年重庆选举基层人大代表期间，韩良作为独立参选人竞选人大代表，遭到当局刁难，后来韩良也因此被拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日“世界人权日”前夕，韩良被当地公安局以“扰乱公共场所秩序”处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日到<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，两天在巴南区民主广场宣传法治，捍卫人权，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日在渝中区奥体广场宣传法治，进行“捍卫人权”的演讲，于<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日失去联系。本网几经周折最近获知韩良已被重庆当局刑事拘留，羁押在渝中区看守所。其辩护权遭剥夺，案情外界不知。后获悉遭秘密审判，判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">4</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、胡光珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，湖北枣阳人，访民领袖。丧偶多年，丈夫和孩子都曾是军人，家住湖北省枣阳市西园三组。因与开发商的拆迁协议纠纷上访，长期以来，胡光珍维权和帮助身边的人维权。曾被拘留<span lang="EN-US">9</span>次，遭不明身份人士非法拘禁<span lang="EN-US">30</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，因在北京上访被地方截访人员遣返原籍，并拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，又被以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘，关押在枣阳第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被转正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日胡光珍案在没有通知近亲家属的情况下开庭，至<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，最终被枣阳市法院以其多次去北京上访告状罪由，以“敲诈勒索罪”判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月刑期。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">5</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、李纪凤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">山东省淄博市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被山东省淄博市警方刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被山东省淄博市中级法院二审维持一审，以利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">6</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、李先利：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川省合江县公民。李先利因在境外服务器创办网站“破楼梦”（<span lang="EN-US">http://polou.me</span>，现已注销），并在上面发表所谓“辱骂、丑化国家领导人、国家机关及国家机关工作人员、丑化党的基本制度的内容”，所以于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被四川合江县警方刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被四川省合江县人民法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。其不服判决，立即提起上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日经四川省泸州市中级人民法院二审裁决，驳回上诉，维持原判。理由是，李先利利用境外服务器开设网站“破楼梦”，从<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月起就先后发表了“从钉子户到部级邪教”、“书记奖金几条被”、“骨灰哪儿去了”、“稻谷仓<span lang="EN-US">8</span>号问题求解”、“<span lang="EN-US">250</span>元人民币漫画”、“泸州九狮山”打油诗、“中国备胎党”等多个文章及图片，由于内容大都涉及丑化、辱骂国家领导人、国家机关及其工作人员，丑化党的基本制度，严重损害了党和国家的形象，并且还通过<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>、微信群，将“破楼梦”网站链接及相应内容、图片直接发给网络好友们分享，破坏了社会秩序，其行为已构成寻衅滋事罪。又因其有前科（李先利曾在<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被合江县人民法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年），须从重处罚，所以二审裁决，依然维持原判。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">7</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、李秀芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省营口市法轮功学员，今年（<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年）<span lang="EN-US">64</span>岁。，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日给营口市站前区东桥派出所、新兴派出所送政府相关文件时被警察非法扣押、构陷，被关押在营口市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日李秀芬遭站前区法院庭审。在法庭上，律师为她做了无罪辩护，李秀芬自己也认为自己无罪（她被非法关押在营口市看守所九个多月）。尽管如此，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月其家属从辩护律师处听说，李秀芬被辽宁省营口市站前区法院<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">8</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、连燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东邹城法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年底连燕在向民众赠送新年台历时，遭人恶告，次日，数十个警察将连燕和丈夫绑架到派出所，几个小时后她的丈夫被放回。连燕被非法关押在枣庄市岳楼看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日上午，济宁市任城区法院人员在枣庄看守所对善良妇女连燕宣判，判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">9</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、林丽芳</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：女，福建省柘荣县人，法轮功学员。曾因信法轮功并参与网上法轮功信息资料接受、传送、现金转帐及宣传等活动，而被宁德市国保人员长期跟踪、蹲点监控。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬，因与肖传雄、金丽燕、陈星光、杨贵媚、杨雄、庄友布、陈开奇、王田等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人先后被宁德市警方抓捕，各人家庭均被查抄，至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其被宁德市检察院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人被福建省宁德市蕉城区法院以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>—<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等，其中林丽芳被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。目前都被关押于福建省宁德市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、刘瑞虎：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1965</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，安徽省阜阳市阜南县人，阜阳市阜南县洪河桥镇曾沃村郑湾东队<span lang="EN-US">28</span>号村民，重型货车司机，网络活跃人士，维权公民，中国在押维权人士。曾因维权多次在各级信访局上访（其中仅安徽省信访局就去过至少<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次），但均毫无效果；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾因中央巡视组在合肥市进行接访，其将申诉材料提交给巡视组，以期得到合理公正的处理结果；却很快被阜南县公安局防暴队及洪河桥镇派出所所长李成抓走，并以在微信里散发对阜南县不利信息为由被拘留<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，曾因在北京向中央信访局递交申诉材料，而被阜南县警方四处追寻，欲用软禁方式阻止其再去北京信访维权<span lang="EN-US">;</span>因其及时逃脱，被迫长期滞留异地，有家不能归；因在网上维权，如发表《村干部的保护伞》、《求救信：基层干部黑暗势力强大，以权栽赃陷害维权人》等文章，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，遂被浙江省里安市公安局马屿派出所警方从里安市京豪酒店以”辱骂和抹黑县领导“为由抓捕，并临时关押在里安市看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，又被移交至安徽省阜南县警方，旋即被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被阜南县检察院以同罪名正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其寻滋案被阜南县检察院向阜南县法院提起公诉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被安徽省阜南县法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；其不服判决，已上诉至安徽省阜南市中级法院；据悉，其妻受连累，在家遭现已辞职的村书记欧打致伤。目前被羁押于阜南县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">11</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、裘小平：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">57</span>岁，湖南长沙人，上世纪八十年代初应召入伍，曾参与”对越自卫反击战”，退伍后被分配到长沙某国有企业工作。除了个人的劳动纠纷，身为退伍军人的裘小平亦积极参与老兵维权活动，多次参与各地老兵维权群体事件以及其他公民维权活动，因此招致长沙当地维稳部门的记恨。裘小平于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月中旬由长沙前往北京维权，在国家人社部等相关部门递交了申告材料后，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日自行返回长沙，在走出长沙火车站时被一早等候的长沙芙蓉区朝阳街道工作人员及朝阳派出所警察等维稳人员强行带走，在做完相关笔录后即被宣布行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天，罪名是“寻衅滋事”和“非法上访”。裘小平拘留届满，警方将裘小平转为刑事拘留，罪名不变，由拘留所转押长沙市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，裘小平案在湖南长沙市芙蓉区法院开庭审理，并被一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">12</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、单丽娜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省阜新市法轮功学员。一个五十几岁的善良妇女，原本拥有一个普通的小家庭，残疾的丈夫离不开她的悉心照顾，在外地读书的孩子离不开她的经济与精神的支持，而今只因她信仰法轮功而遭遇迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，阜新市海州公安分局国保大队闯入单丽娜家中无理抄家，抢走打印机、电脑等私人财物，同时抓捕了单丽娜。单丽娜因身体出现病态，几经周折后由丈夫接回家。后于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被拘捕至阜新市新地看守所，<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日在新地看守所被非法开庭，<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，并勒索罚款五千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">13</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、王好梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省淮阳市法轮功学员。河南省淮阳市东南角小镇鲁台的郑现金、王好梅夫妇，因坚持法轮大法“真善忍”信仰，多次遭绑架、关押，王好梅遭非法劳教，郑现金被判刑八年。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，郑现金、王好梅夫妇第五次被绑架，并都被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，淮阳县城西关法判郑现金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、王好梅<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个。在河南新密监狱，郑现金被迫害的喉管切开，插入管子，维持生命，保外就医回家，将孩子的积蓄都花空了。现在郑现金生活非常困难，只能从胃管里往胃里注射流食。王好梅刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">14</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、吴海波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">广东省湛江市霞山区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日晚在家中被霞山分局国保大队、新村派出所警察绑架；<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被非法逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日遭霞山区法院非法庭审；<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被非法宣判五年徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">15</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、袁琼秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">四川省遂宁市船山区法轮功学员。袁琼秀（<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年六十七岁），<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日上午袁琼秀在家里遭到经开区国保人员及嘉禾派出所警察抓捕、抄家，掠走家中的电脑、刻录机、师父法像、大法书籍等私人物品。后获悉袁琼秀被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被劫持到成都市龙泉驿女子监狱继续关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">16</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、张凤琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">上海法轮功学员。张凤琴于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被上海浦东新区王港派出所绑架后，关押在上海市浦东新区看守所<span lang="EN-US">.2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，张凤琴，被庭审，律师依法驳斥指控。但上海奉贤法院罔顾事实与法律，枉判张凤琴<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">17</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">、钟怡君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁，吉林省长春市人，上海市贝尔公司退休职工，上海市普陀区新村路真金路万里小区居民，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因笃信法轮功，早年曾于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被警方秘密抓捕，之后长期失联，直至半年之后家人才得知她已被逮捕，后被上海市普陀区法院以邪教罪冤判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，但判刑后仍长期下落不明。出狱后，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月初，因其发放法轮功真相资料而再被警方抓捕，失联<span lang="EN-US">1</span>各月后，获悉她被刑拘于上海市普陀区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，其案在上海市普陀区法院开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其被宣判以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。其不服提出上诉，但法院称对其仍然维持原判。目前被关押在上海市普陀区看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
